   35|    821|fn process_syn_stmt(stmt: &mut syn::Stmt, evaluator: &mut Evaluator) -> Result<(), EvalError> {
   36|    821|        match stmt {
   37|    646|            syn::Stmt::Local(local) => {
   38|       |                // Heuristic: If it's a `let` binding, we try to optimize it (Case B).
   39|       |                // If we had `const` or `salt.constant` we would treat it as Case A (Mandatory).
   40|       |                
   41|       |                // For now, scan assignment: let x = <expr>;
   42|       |                // If <expr> evaluates to a constant, register x in the table and replace <expr>.
   43|       |                
   44|    646|                if let Some(init) = &mut local.init {
   45|       |                    // Opportunity: Try to eval
   46|    646|                    match evaluator.eval_expr(&init.expr) {
   47|    103|                        Ok(val) => {
   48|       |                            // It evaluated!
   49|       |                            // 1. Register so future uses can see it (within this scope/flow - simplifying to global for MVP)
   50|    103|                            if let syn::Pat::Ident(pat_ident) = &local.pat {

   54|       |                            // 2. Optimization: Replace the expression with the literal
   55|    103|                            *init.expr = value_to_expr(val);
   56|       |                        },
   57|    543|                        Err(_) => {
   58|    543|                            // Fallback: It's runtime code. Do nothing.
   59|    543|                        }
   60|       |                    }
